/usr/bin/ffmpeg \
-f lavfi -i color=c=black \
-ss 0.000 -t 1.165 \
-i "/var/www/html/public/userfiles/input/r_AUTO_autv1_2019-08-08_09-05-32_54243.mp4" \
-filter_complex " \
[1:v]fps=fps=25[1_fps]; \
[1_fps]scale=1280:720:force_original_aspect_ratio=increase[1_fps_tmpsize]; \
[1_fps_tmpsize]pad=1280:720:x=0:y=0:color=black[1_scaled] \
" \
-map "[1_scaled]" -map "1:a" \
-s 1280x720 \
-aspect 1.777778 \
-r 25 -force_key_frames "expr:gte(t,n_forced*2)" \
-c:v libx264 -b:v 5000k -c:a aac -strict experimental -b:a 128k -f mp4 \
-t 1.165 -async 1 \
-y "/var/www/html/public/userfiles/output/qua/1565974915_5d56e1833237f.mp4"

/usr/bin/ffmpeg \
-f lavfi -i color=c=black \
-ss 0.000 -t 0.711 \
-i "/var/www/html/public/userfiles/input/r_AUTO_autv888_2019-08-08_09-05-32_15623.mp4" \
-filter_complex " \
[1:v]fps=fps=25[1_fps]; \
[1_fps]scale=1280:720:force_original_aspect_ratio=increase[1_fps_tmpsize]; \
[1_fps_tmpsize]pad=1280:720:x=0:y=0:color=black[1_scaled] \
" \
-map "[1_scaled]" -map "1:a" \
-s 1280x720 \
-aspect 1.777778 \
-r 25 -force_key_frames "expr:gte(t,n_forced*2)" \
-c:v libx264 -b:v 5000k -c:a aac -strict experimental -b:a 128k -f mp4 \
-t 0.711 -async 1 \
-y "/var/www/html/public/userfiles/output/hua/1565975428_5d56e384aad58.mp4"
